  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1495a36b-a0eb-4994-b390-7dde9da88c2c'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer14620812145340266364">From <i>USA Today, </i> bestselling author Jillian Dodd comes the third book in the addictive <i>Keatyn Chronicles</i> series. Discover a breathless fairy-tale romance with swoon-worthy characters, suspense, and a glittering celebrity world. Fans of <i>Gossip Girl, Pretty Little Liars</i>, and reality TV will devour this pulse-pounding, sexy teen drama set against the backdrop of Hollywood and</span>
  <span id="freeText14620812145340266364" style="display:none">From <i>USA Today, </i> bestselling author Jillian Dodd comes the third book in the addictive <i>Keatyn Chronicles</i> series. Discover a breathless fairy-tale romance with swoon-worthy characters, suspense, and a glittering celebrity world. Fans of <i>Gossip Girl, Pretty Little Liars</i>, and reality TV will devour this pulse-pounding, sexy teen drama set against the backdrop of Hollywood and an East Coast boarding school. <br /><br />Keatyn’s not scripting her life anymore. She’s living it. She’s done with the God of all Hotties and is going to give her heart to the boy who deserves it. The one whose kisses are hotter than molten lava, who offered her the key to his heart, and who asked her to Homecoming in a big, sexy way. <br /><br />There are so many things to look forward to: parties at the Cave, Homecoming festivities, drama tryouts, and shopping trips to NYC. But things aren’t always as perfect as they seem. She finds out that her best friend has been keeping a secret from her. Not that she can blame him—she has secrets, too. <br /><br />But, for now, she’s going to pretend she’s just a normal girl. She’s going to pretend the stalker’s not still out there, and that he’s not getting more desperate. She’s going to pretend she’ll never see him again. But, she will. And this time, she might not get away. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14620812145340266364" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText11107379455375339147" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>4.5 STARS out of 5<br>Genre: Mature YA-Romance<br>Book 3 in Keatyn Chronicles<br><b> FULL REVIEW POSTED on 4/8/13</b><br><br>Hello my name is Alexis Moore, and I am totally addicted to the Keatyn Chronicles! All I could think when I finished this book was I want<b> MORE MORE MORE!</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380375136ra/729618.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mi5xgpw46p1s2q4bno1_500_zps91bd5f93.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I am in love with Jillian Dodd!!! She get's it right<b>
  <u> EVERY TIME</u>
</b>!!! It's as if she knows my reading taste buds and she cooks up something that knocks my socks off with each installment in this series!!!<br><br>And with the way this book ended... I am positive she is cooking up something<b> G O O D</b> for the next book ,Love Me!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398897ra/771360.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m011t2vCmv1qg395zo1_500_zps37a0a716.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I cannot wait to get my grubby little hands on it!<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398897i/771361.jpg" alt=" photo 00d40045-9f14-4168-8ac1-3f36460e7965_zps8d376702.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398897i/771362.jpg" alt=" photo e5965921-e242-461c-98dc-38041bdb0316_zpsd3fb2d1f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>Boy's Boy's Boy's Boy's<br>Boy's I do adore.....*sighs*</i>
</b><br><b>Kiss me. Date me. Love me. Hate me. STALK ME.</b><br><br><i>'I have the sudden urge to lick him. To see if he tastes as good as he looks. He leans back to watch the next audition, taking his big hand with him. I close my eyes and shake my head. How the hell does he do that? Damn, him! He's like a god damn walking love potion.'</i> ~Keatyn<br><br>I am ABSOLUTELY 100% head over heels in love with Keatyn. Even when she makes mistakes I love her because it just shows that shes human. This book picked up right where kiss me left off. Keatyn is riding her high on cloud nine after just being asked publicly by Dawson to go to Homecoming. She graciously accepts of course! It’s not long before Dawson and Keatyn decide to become an official couple and things are good for them.. Really really good! ***wiggles eyebrows suggestively***<br><br><i>'Dawson is like a sexual buffet. I never know what to expect, what’s going to be next in line. But I definitely want to keep going back for more.'</i> ~Keatyn<br><br>Dawson definitely knows how to bring the sex appeal an while I enjoyed it, it also would have been nice for him to get know Keatyn on a deeper level. I mean damn their whole relationship was physical. On the other hand I felt Aiden connected with Keatyn in this book on a more personal level. It almost seemed as if Aiden was purposely aiming to get to know Keatyn in a more personal way. He wanted to understand her and her reasoning behind some of the choices she has made. I liked that. I am not sure who I want Keatyn to end up with I love both Dawson and Aiden. Yes, I love Keatyn and Dawson together but I think Aiden is<b> “the one”</b> however only time will tell. <br><br>Ok so here are the <b>HIGHLIGHTS</b> in no particular order<br><br><b>-A couple makes it official <br>–Someone gets the key to a boys heart<br>–Someone is kissing other guys not just her boyfriend<br>-Whitney is up to no good <br>–Someone cashes in their V card <br>–Someone cheats <br>-Someone drops a <u>BOMB</u> by revealing a secret <br>–Someone else.. cheats <br>–There is a school Break-in..or something like that *wink,wink*<br>–Drunk texting <br>–Someone meets the parents <br>-Whitney is still up to no good<br>–Good times are had in New York City <br>-There is a Vincent siting <br>–Certain someones make a video on a private jet that goes viral <br>–<u>ANOTHER</u> secret is revealed <br>–Someone finds out it was written in the stars</b><br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br>Keatyn has been cautiously guarding her heart, shes made bad decisions in the past and she does not want to experience that heartbreak again. I love the talk she had with her mom. It was so heartfelt, I love to see a mother daughter relationship that is open and honest. Keatyn’s friendship with Riley and Dallas priceless. Those two have Keatyn’s back no matter what! I loved getting to meet Dawson’s brothers, Braxton had me laughing so hard I had stomach cramps. Cannot wait to get more of him!<br>You did it again Jillian Dodd! I CANNOT WAIT to read LOVE ME!!!!<br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Lovable<br>Writing Style- Fun, Witty, and Savory<br>Plot/Storyline- Unputdownable, and fast paced with a touch of Suspense<br>Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy<br>Overall- I LOVED IT! READ IT!!<br><br>Warning: This book has mature content and is best suited for readers 16 and older.<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a><br><br>*Copy kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review*<br><br><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16900961540176816052"><b>On to the next one for my re-read! LOVE IT!!!!</b><br/><br/><br/><b>5 BoyCrazy Stars!!!!! </b><br/><br/><u>THESE BOOKS ARE LIKE CRACK TO ME! </u>Seriously... I can’t get enough! <br/><br/>I love Keatyn and all her boys... I feel like a boy crazy book hussy while reading, but I’m okay with that!!! Not even sure where to start on this review, but I’ll start with the obvious... THE BOYS<br/><br/><b>GOD OF ALL HOTTIES:</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/Dateme-Aidredone_zps1fefab27.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Aiden... You used your god powers on me and now I am on your side! Aiden was pretty irresistible in this book. I loved him at the end of Stalk M</span>
  <span id="freeText16900961540176816052" style="display:none"><b>On to the next one for my re-read! LOVE IT!!!!</b><br><br><br><b>5 BoyCrazy Stars!!!!! </b><br><br><u>THESE BOOKS ARE LIKE CRACK TO ME! </u>Seriously... I can’t get enough! <br><br>I love Keatyn and all her boys... I feel like a boy crazy book hussy while reading, but I’m okay with that!!! Not even sure where to start on this review, but I’ll start with the obvious... THE BOYS<br><br><b>GOD OF ALL HOTTIES:</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/Dateme-Aidredone_zps1fefab27.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Aiden... You used your god powers on me and now I am on your side! Aiden was pretty irresistible in this book. I loved him at the end of Stalk Me, during Kiss Me, not so much... Now this book- I love him again! I think everyone BUT Keatyn knew how Aiden felt about her. I just wish he would have made his feelings for her clearer earlier...<br><br><b>MR. GORGEOUS: </b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/Dateme-Dawesredone_zps2ba25dc2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398887i/771298.jpg" alt=" photo Dateme-Dawesredone_zps2ba25dc2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don’t even know where to start with Dawson... I loved you so much, I was rooting for you, and you let me down. You don’t tell someone they own you and then make a crap decision like that... just saying. Maybe he can redeem himself down the line, maybe not. Only time will tell.<br><br><b>RILEY</b><br> My absolute FAVORITE! I just love Riley. I love how sweet and protective he is of Keatyn. I love that he calls her baby, is always there for her and always takes her side. I especially loved <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[That he slept on her floor for a few nights because he was worried about V coming. If Keats can tell anyone her big secret, I think Riley would be it. Freaking love him!!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>My favorite Riley line:<br><i> Every guy at school is sitting around simultaneously thinking what a dumb fuck you are and thanking you for being one. I’m out.</i><br><br><b>DALLAS</b><br>I also really like Dallas. He is a funny and sweet guy and a good friend to Keatyn. We learn more about Dallas in this book. If anything, he can relate more to Keatyn than anyone. <br>My Dallas line:<br><i>She’s way too high strung for me. It was like dating Tigger with boobs.</i><br><br><b>DAMIEN</b><br> I was SO HAPPY to get some Damien in this book! I’ve missed him. One of Keatyn’s oldest friends. I could definitely see Damien and Keatyn together in the future... <br><i>You were my Keatie first</i><br><br>I know I am leaving out a ton of guys... We also meet Dawson and Riley’s older brother Cam, and younger brother Braxton (loved that kid!) and of course there is Jake. He is a sweetheart.<br><br>There is so much going on in Date Me, its hard to even summarize... <br>Homecoming is the big thing. Keatyn makes friends with Peyton and frienemies with Whitney. Vincent makes a few guest appearances. Keats tries out for the school play. There is a lot of dancing. There is heartbreak and cheating. There are four leaf clovers and glow in the dark stars.<br><br>Now to the main attraction:  <br><b>KEATIE</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/Dateme-Keatieredone_zpse4b90651.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398887i/771299.jpg" alt=" photo Dateme-Keatieredone_zpse4b90651.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I absolutely love Keatyn! Couldn’t love her more! She is growing up and trying to be smart and make good decisions. I can’t wait to see where her journey takes us in ‘Love Me.’<br><br>Some of my FAVORITE Keatyn lines: <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I put my hands on top of his and move them around my body in the name of dancing.<br>This would be even funner if we were naked.<br>Shit.<br>Hello? You can’t think that.<br><br>“I’m not dating Dawson to be popular, Whitney. I’m dating him for hot sex.”<br><br>Aiden lets out a deep, sexy growl. The kind of growl that makes a girl want to rip off her panties. <br>Not me, of course. I’m just saying most girls. Well, some girls would, maybe.<br>I think. <br><br>Electrical shivers shoot up my leg.<br>And my knee is such a slut!<br> She likes it!<br> She’s that friend you have. The one who you tell you’re on a diet and the next day she shows up with cupcakes and says, Aww, just one won’t hurt.<br><br>“I was going to say that you’re doing a great job. With the hammer. With the, uh, hammering. Like, you seem to be pretty good at hammering. Uh, I mean pounding. Or, um, nailing. You know, whatever its called.”<br><br>Oh yeah, I’m going to like being single.  Welcome to my whoredom, boys...</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>Now I have to ask the million dollar question... Aiden or Dawson???<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/Dateme-bootsredone_zpsb71e1742.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398887i/771300.jpg" alt=" photo Dateme-bootsredone_zpsb71e1742.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398887i/771301.jpg" alt=" photo DateMe-Daweskissredone_zps9bd4552a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  If Dawson has the potential to break my heart, crack it in two, Aiden has the power to annihilate it.
</b><br>At the end of this book I am 100% <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[TEAM AIDEN- how can you not be after that ending?!?!?!? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I know this review has been all over the place. But I really just LOVE these books. They are funny, sweet, sexy and just all around awesome. If you get one thing from this, just know<br><b>THIS SERIES IS A MUST READ!!!!!</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer710882942" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18284809487022072866"><br/><b>4.5 "I am 100% addicted to this series" STARS.</b><br/><p><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435412ra/879633.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Yep, this series just keeps getting better and better and I'm loving every second of it! Jillian Dodd is fast becoming one of my new favorite authors! These books are fun, entertaining, fast-paced and a little over-the-top, but that's exactly what I like about them. There is never a dull moment in Keatyn's life and that's what makes these books so damn good and just unputdownable!<br/><br/><u><b>Random thought and highlights:</b> (might contain spoilers)</u><br/><br/>❥ <b>Aiden's hidden</b></p></span>
  <span id="freeText18284809487022072866" style="display:none"><br><b>4.5 "I am 100% addicted to this series" STARS.</b><br><p><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435412ra/879633.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Yep, this series just keeps getting better and better and I'm loving every second of it! Jillian Dodd is fast becoming one of my new favorite authors! These books are fun, entertaining, fast-paced and a little over-the-top, but that's exactly what I like about them. There is never a dull moment in Keatyn's life and that's what makes these books so damn good and just unputdownable!<br><br><u><b>Random thought and highlights:</b> (might contain spoilers)</u><br><br>❥ <b>Aiden's hidden dance "talent"</b> and Kaetyn's reaction to it:<br><br></p><blockquote>
  <i>"What the hell? Do you used to be in a boy band? Are you here in some embarrassment protection program?"</i>
</blockquote><br>❥ <b>Keatyn accepting the necklace with the key to Dawson's heart.</b><br>❥ <b>Keatyn tutoring French to Aiden</b> and the dirty talking in French that goes with it.<br>❥ <b>Damian's Rock Star song.</b> *SWOON*<br>❥ <b>Shopping trips to New York</b> and crazy car chases.<br>❥ <b>The Mission: Impossible Party.</b><br>❥ <b>Late nights at The Cave with Dallas and Riley.</b><br>❥ <b>Homecoming.</b> <br>❥ <b>Run-ins with Vincent.</b> Not so much fun... That guy keeps getting crazier and crazier :S.<br>❥ <b>The crazy, hilarious music video with Dallas and Riley.</b><br>❥ <b>Keatyn *finally* finding out the truth about Aiden's stars for Homecoming. </b> <br><br><blockquote>
<i>"I did it because I think it's time you finally knew the stars were always for you. Always. Only. Ever. For you."</i> ♥♥</blockquote><br><br>I feel like I could go on and on about these books, but all I'm going to say is: If you haven't read this series yet and you're looking for a fun, addictive, hilarious, sweet story, then READ it!! You won't regret it ;-).<br><br><br>♦<u>
  <b>My casting for Keatyn, Dawson &amp; Aiden:</b>
</u>♦<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435412i/879634._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435413i/879635._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435413i/879636.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At the beginning, I was 90% sure I was Team Dawson BUT then he went ahead and did some things that I could NOT approve of. So, from now on I think I'm going to be Team Aiden. To me, he seems like the best match for Keatyn and he just keeps saying the sweetest things to her. <br><br>But of course I love all the other boys in Keatyn's life too: Riley, Dallas, Damian, Jake, Camden, Brooklyn...and last but not least, the newest addition to the Johnson brothers clan: Braxton! Only 14 years old but already a true player...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Braxton: Right now, I'd like a trio of slutty girls. All naked together in my room with nothing to do but me.<br><br>Keatyn: Let's try to deal with reality.<br><br>Braxton: I was. I originally wanted a harem.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>See what I mean? LOL! I'm really glad with all the new characters the author keeps introducing in every new book and I can't wait to read much more of this series and Kaetyn's crazy, exciting new adventures! <br><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3969447648884331975"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408134820i/10811883._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>I will begin with the end…WOW! I freaking loved this ending! That’s all you will get out of me, because I am a <i>Glitter Whore</i> not a <i>Spoiler Whore.</i><br/><br/><b>Date Me</b> picks up where <b>Kiss Me</b> leaves off. Keatyn begins dating Dawson, and is quickly becoming the <i>it girl</i> at school. She is learning that she has to live her life not script it. <br/><br/>I love Keatyn! Basically Keatyn is having to grow up pretty quickly. She has been emancipated, has excess to her trust fund, and can basically go and do whatever she</span>
  <span id="freeText3969447648884331975" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!!!</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408134820i/10811883._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I will begin with the end…WOW! I freaking loved this ending! That’s all you will get out of me, because I am a <i>Glitter Whore</i> not a <i>Spoiler Whore.</i><br><br><b>Date Me</b> picks up where <b>Kiss Me</b> leaves off. Keatyn begins dating Dawson, and is quickly becoming the <i>it girl</i> at school. She is learning that she has to live her life not script it. <br><br>I love Keatyn! Basically Keatyn is having to grow up pretty quickly. She has been emancipated, has excess to her trust fund, and can basically go and do whatever she wants but chooses to be responsible. She is a good friend and always takes up for the underdog. She uses her popularity for good not evil, like that bitch Whitney. I also love that Keatyn is just like every other teenage girl. Her emotions are spot on, she gets upset she is over emotional and falls in love quickly…but that just makes the story more real to me. <br><br>This story has a little bit of suspense and shocking moments, it has swoon worthy moments, and all together it makes you feel good. I am <b>LOVING</b> The Keatyn Chronicles and have my book-mate to thank for turning me on to them. <br><br><b>I am still team God of all Hotties!!</b><br><br>Again I listened to the audiobook for this one, and I love the narrator!</span>

    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11335012431633357562"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400338i/775611.jpg' width='375' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Jillian Dodd has created such an addicting series in the Keatyn Chronicles. Lots and Lots of boys! <br/><br/>If you have read the series and are up to Date Me, you will be swooning, laughing, and quite possibly have to pick your jaw off the floor all the while enjoying every page of this book. <br/><br/>I was Team Dawson up until this book. Yes I was drinking the Johnson Brother’s Kool Aid a</span>
  <span id="freeText11335012431633357562" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400338i/775611.jpg" width="375" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Jillian Dodd has created such an addicting series in the Keatyn Chronicles. I can't get enough of these books. They are all about growing up, having lots of fun, wearing fabulous clothes and hot boys! Lots and Lots of boys! <br><br>If you have read the series and are up to Date Me, you will be swooning, laughing, and quite possibly have to pick your jaw off the floor all the while enjoying every page of this book. <br><br>I was Team Dawson up until this book. Yes I was drinking the Johnson Brother’s Kool Aid and loving it. I was so prepared for Keatyn to take that necklace and fall for Dawson. I will not spoil the story so I’ll just that I’m still recovering... someone spilled my Kool Aid!<br><br>What about the God of All Hotties? I like him don’t get me wrong, he is sweet and yeah hot and a bit vague when he talks to her. I find him a bit frustrating and skittish.<br><br>After finishing Date Me, I’m still drinking the Kool Aid and I’m all about <b>TEAM RILEY</b>!!! I can’t say enough about him. He is loyal, protective and absolutely hilarious. I smile every time Riley and Keatyn are together.<br> <br>Bottom line, this book was a great read! Vincent is still lurking, Keatyn pursues her acting ambitions, participates so really fun school events while making friends and following her heart!<br><br>I loved the ending and I’m more than excited to read Love Me!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11353671884852540394"><b>Curve balls to the heart and a drug test...</b><br/><br/>I’m seriously thinking about having The Keatyn Chronicles drug tested. No seriously. If I made it pee words in a cup, it would come back positive. <br/><br/>It's like Jillian Dodd laced this series with heroine, I'm addicted. Everything about what's going on...the guys....the indecision. It drives me bat shit crazy, but I can't get ENOUGH!!! <br/><br/>This book picks up exactly where <i>Kiss Me</i> left off. And just like its predecessors, it drove me insane, completely insane. E</span>
  <span id="freeText11353671884852540394" style="display:none"><b>Curve balls to the heart and a drug test...</b><br /><br />I’m seriously thinking about having The Keatyn Chronicles drug tested. No seriously. If I made it pee words in a cup, it would come back positive. <br /><br />It's like Jillian Dodd laced this series with heroine, I'm addicted. Everything about what's going on...the guys....the indecision. It drives me bat shit crazy, but I can't get ENOUGH!!! <br /><br />This book picks up exactly where <i>Kiss Me</i> left off. And just like its predecessors, it drove me insane, completely insane. Even the parts you don’t like, you tolerate, and the parts you hate, you love. It’s a crazy addiction that I can’t explain. <br /><br />For us Team Dawsoners, he was…how do I put this? Very much about the sex and less about the love. Aiden got all the quality conversations, and deep moments. Don’t get me wrong, Dawson was still sexy, sweet, and caring, but he breathed sex. He showed his love in a very physical way. I’m still Team Dawson though!! TEAM DAWSON....and his penis!!<br /><br />Despite my devotion for Team Dawson; it officially has some alternates now. Dallas and Riley won me over in a big way. Especially Riley. I absolutely love them. LOVE!!<br /><br />If I’m going to be completely honest though, this book scared me. I’m afraid of what happened…what’s to come. So much unknown. So much speculation. So much confusion. I want what I want and I’m afraid it may go in another direction. I’m afraid to be hit in the heart with a curve ball. However, it’s the fact that I care so damn much that shows just how truly unique and addictive this series is. If you haven’t read The Keatyn Chronicles, GO! NOW! <br /><br />READ ON!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_499604594" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/499604594" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/499604594?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer499604594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18114339653649518584"><a href='http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/2013/04/blog-tour-date-me-by-jillian-dodd.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>This Review was Posted at Angie's Dreamy Reads!</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>4 FABULOUS TEAM KIKI STARS</i>
</b><br/><br/>I just <b>ADORE</b> this series. <b>EVERYTHING</b> about the Keatyn Chronicles rocks my world. Jillian's writing is absolutely addicting. I devoured this book in less than <b>ONE</b> day!! Once I started it was impossible to put down! The drama, angst and sexiness is a total blast to read. I have to say that I'm sad and a little heartbroken that I am no longer a Team Dawson girl. Ugh...I can't even believe that I'm saying that!! In book two</span>
  <span id="freeText18114339653649518584" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/2013/04/blog-tour-date-me-by-jillian-dodd.html" rel="nofollow noopener">This Review was Posted at Angie's Dreamy Reads!</a><br /><br /><b>
  <i>4 FABULOUS TEAM KIKI STARS</i>
</b><br /><br />I just <b>ADORE</b> this series. <b>EVERYTHING</b> about the Keatyn Chronicles rocks my world. Jillian's writing is absolutely addicting. I devoured this book in less than <b>ONE</b> day!! Once I started it was impossible to put down! The drama, angst and sexiness is a total blast to read. I have to say that I'm sad and a little heartbroken that I am no longer a Team Dawson girl. Ugh...I can't even believe that I'm saying that!! In book two, Kiss Me, I was <b>ALL</b> about Dawson. He was so sweet and adorable. I thought there was nothing a girl wouldn't love about him. I’m sad to say that he crushed me and I'm now lost. Totally lost. Which team do I go for now because the pool of amazing boys are plenty. Riley, Aiden, Jake, Dallas....I could go on and on and on. There are so many delicious, sweet and lovable character that Jillian has created for us to love. I really think it’s incredible that all these characters have snuck their way into our hearts one way or another. I’m telling you this series is so good. I’m not a big high school age, YA book fan! I’m just not but there is something about this series that will hook you and keep you coming back for more and more!! <b>AND</b> the best part is that every single book just gets better and better. I love it. <br /><br />In Date Me we pick up right where we left off in the last book. I don’t want to go into the whole plot of what happens just in case you haven’t read the series but it’s <b>SOOOOOOO</b> good. Keatyn is with Dawson and is still fighting a <b>BIG</b> crush on “The God of all hotties” aka Aiden. Dawson has just won her over and wooed her in an <b>EPIC</b> way, that leaves her feeling on top of the world. She learns in Date Me that sometimes love stinks and that boys can be stupid. She still has to deal with crazy, scary Vincent, who again makes a couple appearances that left me freaked out. SO much happens in this book. I want to tell you it all but I can’t! I just can’t ruin it for those who haven’t read the first two in the series. <br /><br />Overall I think I fell in love with Aiden and I’m back to being on his <b>TEAM</b> all the way. I’m trying to mend my broken heart from a certain boy who has crushed it and find myself rooting hard for Keatyn to find some kind of true love, as well as, some freedom to just live her life freely and not in fear. I would say to you if you haven’t read this series or are thinking about it, <b>READ</b> IT!!!! You’ll love it. There’s something so fun and refreshing about each and everyone of these amazing characters. Once you start reading, you’ll be a Jillian Dodd fan for life. It’s so good. <b>SO, SO, SO</b> good. If you <b>HAVE</b> read the first two in the series, you can expect some angst and laughs. I know at the end of this you’ll be even more in love with Keatyn and her posse. I can't wait for the next book in the series Love Me.<br /><br />MY BLOG LINK --&gt;&gt; <a href="http://www.angiesdreamyreads.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Angie's Dreamy Reads</a><br /><br />BLOG FACEBOOK LINK ---&gt;&gt; <a href="https://www.facebook.com/AngiesDreamyReads" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook - Angie's Dreamy Reads</a></span>

    <a title="Autumn Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6908049-autumn-review"><img alt="Autumn Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1399327915p2/6908049.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/487014785?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Autumn Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Autumn Review" href="/user/show/6908049-autumn-review">Autumn Review</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6908049-autumn-review?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer487014785" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4842773491148100377">I'm a mother. I'm married. I'm THIRTY-FIVE years old!!! So, why am I acting like my heart has been crushed like a high school girls'??? I'll tell you why: Jillian Dodd did this. She's officially made me into an indecisive, silly girl about all these luscious boys. In order not to spoil this book, I thought it would be best to give you, the reader, a break down of the boys from this particular book. You see, we know all the players at this point, but some of the game has changed. Some of these bo</span>
  <span id="freeText4842773491148100377" style="display:none">I'm a mother. I'm married. I'm THIRTY-FIVE years old!!! So, why am I acting like my heart has been crushed like a high school girls'??? I'll tell you why: Jillian Dodd did this. She's officially made me into an indecisive, silly girl about all these luscious boys. In order not to spoil this book, I thought it would be best to give you, the reader, a break down of the boys from this particular book. You see, we know all the players at this point, but some of the game has changed. Some of these boys could be potential suitors, some are just friends. If you are a fan of this series, you know what I'm talking about. Yes, yes...some have your "team" and you're ready to settle with that but me, I'm not so sure yet. Let me show you why.<br /><br />First up is Riley. Riley is funny, sweet, and truly a great friend to Keatyn. When Keatie first met Riley, he was definitely a player. Now, he's crushing on one particular girl. Despite his own love life, he is always there for Keatyn. They really do have a great friendship. She is open and honest with him as much as she can be. I really love Riley. However, I don't think he's Moon Boy.<br /><br />Next is Dallas. I have to say that I would be happy if Keatyn and Dallas ended up together. I think Dallas would have a really good understanding of what Keatyn is going through. Being the son of a politician has certainly put him in some interesting situations, so I think he could be a good support to Keatie. Dallas makes me laugh, but there is a vulnerability to him that makes him endearing.<br /><br />Aiden has been touch and go for me. Sure, he's sexy, hot, and in this book....I'll admit, he won me over a little bit. Just a smidge. Even though Aiden hasn't been forthcoming in his feelings for Keatie, I've never doubted his true intentions with her. When I first met him though, I thought he was just kind of cocky and kind of jerky. In Date Me, I felt like he was really ready to put it all out there. Would I be disappointed if he was Moon Boy? Not anymore. I'm warming to the idea.<br /><br />Dawson. Oh Dawson. Is there anything left to say? What can I say? Hmmm....Ok, how about this: Dawson hurt me in this book. I fell in love with this boy in Kiss Me. I mean, I was ready to start planning a wedding here. Dawson is hot. He's likable. I always thought he and Keatie (me) were a great match. Now, I'm just not sure. He's made some bad choices and I just don't see how it could be possible for him to be Moon Boy. *cries*<br /><br />Finally, Damien. I'm still holding out for Damien. I absolutely love him. In my mind, he's still her constant. They've known each other since they were little and I think he really loves Keatyn. That said, I do think it's good that they are both experiencing what life has to offer right now. Even if Keatyn's life has been forced on her. In the end, I hope that Damien could be the man of Keatie's dreams. Time will tell.<br /><br />Overall, I really liked Date Me. I will go as far to say that this book has been my favorite in the series so far. There is some drama with Vincent. Even though Keatyn's love life usually takes center stage, the danger she's in does still have a major role in the overall plot. Must not forget that. I'm really anxious for Love Me. I loved the ending of this one and can't wait to see how the story is going to play out in the next book. Are you a fan of NA Contemporaries? Do you like reading about hot guys? Then, yes...this is a great series for you.<br /><br />Quotes:<br />~"What the hell?" I say, shocked. "Did you used to be in a boy band? Are you here in some embarrassment protection program?"-Loc 399/ARC<br /><br />~"You know, Mom. You taught me all about protection and how not to get pregnant, but never once did you teach me how to protect my heart."-Loc 612/ARC<br /><br />~"You own me. You know that, right? Totally and completely own me."-Loc 4749/ARC</span>

<div id="review_464874451" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/464874451" />
    <a title="Melissa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9119769-melissa"><img alt="Melissa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1335615404p2/9119769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/464874451?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melissa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melissa" href="/user/show/9119769-melissa">Melissa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer464874451" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8467348651824371750">I was extremely privileged to be part of the Beta Team for Date Me and the following is an unbiased spoiler free review.<br/><br/>The thing that makes me nervous when reading an instalment of a book series that I love is that it wont measure up to the previous books . I always worry that it will be a case of 'one book too many' and characters that i have grown to love will be placed in unrealistic situations just to fill word quotas. Well I can rest easy because Date Me is NOT one of those books and if an</span>
  <span id="freeText8467348651824371750" style="display:none">I was extremely privileged to be part of the Beta Team for Date Me and the following is an unbiased spoiler free review.<br /><br />The thing that makes me nervous when reading an instalment of a book series that I love is that it wont measure up to the previous books . I always worry that it will be a case of 'one book too many' and characters that i have grown to love will be placed in unrealistic situations just to fill word quotas. Well I can rest easy because Date Me is NOT one of those books and if anything it actually EXCEEDED my expectations in storyline, character development and a few additions that were VERY UNEXPECTED!<br /><br />Date me picks up perfectly where Kiss Me left us with Keatyn accepting Dawson's invitation to Homecoming and me wondering why no boy ever put stars on his ceiling to ask me out ?!?! While i must admit I chose what boy was my favourite early on in this series, there are quite a few moments in DATE ME when my allegiances were questioned by some rather sweet and very swoon worthy moments by a certain other boy ! OK there were some rather HOT moments in there as well , but I am only human so do not judge me !!!!<br /><br />Once again Date Me is set over a very short time frame and Jillian Dodds pacing of this book is to perfection and the content selection is so concise that there just isn't any moments that you would consider to be irrelevant . We meet new characters and get a lot of back stories on the existing characters that will give you quite a few ..'Oh , now I know why that happened' moments .<br /><br />So in Date Me we have moments of pure hilarity with the entry of the youngest Johnson brother . We welcome wisecracking and future King of the Whoredom Braxton. He really gives Dallas a run for his money and I can see we are going to be really good friends through out this series.<br /><br />We have some really scary moments . Hi Vincent nice to see you again ....NOT !!<br /><br />We have some moments that will melt your heart, make you reach for a tissue and say to yourself If Keatyn doesn't want you , look me up .... Yes Aiden , I'm talking to you ;)<br /><br />Oh and the friendship dynamics between Keatyn , Riley and Dallas !! WOW they had some moments that were right up there with my favourites ...EVER. <br /><br />And lets not forget how MY HEART WAS BROKEN !!! SMASHED, SHREDDED !!! And in steps angst !!! Thank you very much ... you know who you are and btw we are NOT friends at the moment !!!!!<br /><br />And lastly ... Keatyn , I am quite proud of our little protagonist ... She is making better choices, making some great friends and finally beginning to know and like herself. YAY !! <br /><br /><br />So basically what I am trying to say ,and successfully I hope, is that I LOVED THIS BOOK . Its definitely my favourite in the series so far . 5+ stars . If you are a fan of The Keatyn Chronicles this book will ROCK YOUR WORLD , yep true story. Oh and the ending, OMG if it doesn't make you look for another page or shake your kindle in hope for just a little bit more , then seriously you need to give up reading FOREVER . <br /><br />Well done Jillian Dodd ...Brilliant</span>
  <a data-text-id="8467348651824371750" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_503023603" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/503023603" />
    <a title="Paula " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2879703-paula"><img alt="Paula " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536687412p2/2879703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/503023603?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula " href="/user/show/2879703-paula">Paula </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer503023603" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16826559813244839699"><br/><i>Date Me</i> is absolutely magically delicious and my favorite in this series so far. It picks up exactly where <i>Kiss Me</i> ended. Keatyn has just been asked to Homecoming by Dawson in one of the most exciting and original ways. She’s floating on ‘Dawson cloud nine’ and has finally decided to accept the ‘key to his heart’ that will make them official. Life is good for this couple. They have fun together and they have FUN together – if you know what I mean. Keatyn has finally found a good group of friends</span>
  <span id="freeText16826559813244839699" style="display:none"><br /><i>Date Me</i> is absolutely magically delicious and my favorite in this series so far. It picks up exactly where <i>Kiss Me</i> ended. Keatyn has just been asked to Homecoming by Dawson in one of the most exciting and original ways. She’s floating on ‘Dawson cloud nine’ and has finally decided to accept the ‘key to his heart’ that will make them official. Life is good for this couple. They have fun together and they have FUN together – if you know what I mean. Keatyn has finally found a good group of friends. She’s involved in school functions and is going to try out for the school play. Things are going great in Keatyn’s world. Sort of. <br /><br />My little Keatie has really grown up quite a bit since I first met her in <i>Stalk Me</i>. She’s coming into her own. She knows what she wants in life and is ready to pursue it. But, like any teenager, she makes mistakes and bad decisions. I love Keatyn. She marches to her own drum. She’s a fun chick with a huge heart. However, she does have a lot on her plate as she struggles with missing her family and old friends while still dealing with the psycho stalker, Vincent. That’s a lot for any seventeen year old girl to handle. However, Keatyn is not one to sit around and moan about her life. She may have a break down every once in a while, but she gets back up and continues to dance to her own beat, making the best of everything. The girl has a heart of gold. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“I’m not dating Dawson to be popular, Whitney. I’m dating him for hot sex.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Despite her worries over her stalker, she definitely has it good with two hot guys vying for her attention. I fell pretty hard for Dawson in <i>Kiss Me</i>. He’s a good guy, playful, and meltingly sexy. Sure, Dawson and Keatyn have a lot of fun together, and really good sexual chemistry, but I feel like Dawson never tried to get to know Keatyn on a more personal level besides the physical part. The eighteen year old horny teenager in Dawson came out full force in this book – among other things. Dawson needs a swift kick in the hiny. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>Aiden lets out a deep, sexy growl. The kind of growl that makes a girl want to rip off her panties. <br />Not me, of course. I’m just saying most girls. Well, some girls would, maybe. <br />I think..</b>
</i><br /><br />And then there is Aiden, who I had big issues with in <i>Kiss Me</i>, yet he completely surprised me in a very good way in this installment. In the last book, I wasn’t willing to look at Aiden as anything more than an annoying nat buzzing around Dawson and Keatyn’s relationship. But then, all of a sudden, I immediately felt the connection between Aiden and Keatyn, and I saw just how compatible they are together. Aiden showed me how thoughtful, passionate, and swoon-worthy he really is. Now, I have to agree with Keatyn, Aiden really is the God of all Hotties. I was wooed.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>If Dawson has the potential to break my heart, crack it in two, Aiden has the power to annihilate it.</b>
</i> <br /><br />When I first started this story, I was adamant to remain loyal to Team Dawson. Then, suddenly I found myself switching gears 8% into the book. My heart started swooning for someone else. And then my head was spinning with disbelief that I could be wooed that quickly. I don’t know who Keatyn will end up with. I’m not even sure I’m ready to give up on Dawson. He’s not a bad guy, he’s just young and slightly immature. Could Dawson or Aiden be the one? Who knows. Miz Dodd is tricky when it comes to the hot male leads in Keatyn’s life. I have to give Jillian Dodd kudos. She has an amazing writing talent where you will become emotionally and passionately attached to her characters. She has a way with creating a character and showing you what she wants you to see at the moment. And then she will open that character up and show you their true colors. I’m definitely impressed by Miz Dodd’s writing skill, indeed. <br /><br />I adore the secondary characters in this story, especially Dallas and Riley. I admit to having a huge crush on both of them. They both make me laugh and smile. And the fact they both protect and love Keatyn like family would is truly awe-worthy. Part of me thinks that Keatyn will end up with Dallas at some point. But, maybe that’s wishful thinking on my part. And then there is Damian. The super, sexy rock star has piqued my interest. Oh, yes. Miz Dodd has me in hot boy overload again. <br /><br />I love this series, the characters, the storyline, everything. The Keatyn Chronicles is addictive, to put it mildly. I never thought I could get so emotionally involved in a tween series, but this series certainly has my undivided and devoted attention. The twist at the end of Date Me was freaking fantastic. Keatyn has some decisions to make and I cannot wait to see what happens in <i>Love Me</i>!<br /><br />Rating: B+<br />Heat: Sweet<br /><br /><br />-- <i>A <a href="http://romanticbookaffairs.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Romantic Book Affairs</a> Review</i><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Find us on <a href="https://twitter.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> and <a href="http://facebook.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> too!</i>
</b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16826559813244839699" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText13152062533967507927" style="display:none"><b>"Haven't you ever seen a movie where two people are supposed to fall in love but you just can't picture them together? Seriously it was that good!!! <br /><br /><b>"Ha!               <span id="reviewTextContainer480941721" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7034944510665607291">Review posted to: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Swept Away By Romance</a><br/><br/><b>5 Stars<br/>Genre: Contemporary, MATURE Young Adult/New Adult Romance<br/>Heat Barometer: 4 out of 5 flames</b><br/><br/>I am totally addicted to this series and I will be counting down the days until August 15th and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16401102.Love_Me__The_Keatyn_Chronicles___4_' title='Love Me (The Keatyn Chronicles, #4) by Jillian Dodd' rel='nofollow noopener'>Love Me</a>, book #4 becomes available. It is a <i>Gossip Girl</i> series of the rich, spoiled and over indulgent youth. Some have great character and some have great flaws, but they are typical teenagers filled with love, lust, fickleness, and consistent ability to make stupid </span>
  <span id="freeText7034944510665607291" style="display:none">Review posted to: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Swept Away By Romance</a><br /><br /><b>5 Stars<br />Genre: Contemporary, MATURE Young Adult/New Adult Romance<br />Heat Barometer: 4 out of 5 flames</b><br /><br />I am totally addicted to this series and I will be counting down the days until August 15th and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16401102.Love_Me__The_Keatyn_Chronicles___4_" title="Love Me (The Keatyn Chronicles, #4) by Jillian Dodd" rel="nofollow noopener">Love Me</a>, book #4 becomes available. It is a <i>Gossip Girl</i> series of the rich, spoiled and over indulgent youth. Some have great character and some have great flaws, but they are typical teenagers filled with love, lust, fickleness, and consistent ability to make stupid decisions. <br /><br />This is what I would describe as a guilty pleasure for me because I feel guilty due to the fact that I don't agree with Keatyn's morals, especially at such a young age, she is a little free and easy with the sex. Her sex life, the party scene, and the access these kids have to this wild lifestyle is outrageous, BUT I love reading about it. Also the parenting situation is a little disturbing to me too. Not because she doesn't have a loving family situation, but I just feel conflicted because Keatyn really needs to be with her superstar parents. She emancipated herself in book 1, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13557124.Stalk_Me__The_Keatyn_Chronicles___1_" title="Stalk Me (The Keatyn Chronicles, #1) by Jillian Dodd" rel="nofollow noopener">Stalk Me</a> because she was running from a crazy stalker and her being around her famous family could jeopardize their security. Tommy, her stepfather (think Brad Pitt) and her mom (more Jennifer Anniston than Angelina) need to protect her and direct her. That being said you wouldn't have the wild ride that is a blast to follow in these books.<br /><br />In the series Keatyn goes through many different relationships and loves, some turn out good, some not so, but I was totally enthralled with each one as they progress. The character Keatyn is fun and a great friend to many. I just love all the interactions and hook ups between the large cast of characters. The love story and the love triangle in <b>Date Me</b> is hot and gets my blood pumping. Dawson is great, but Aidan is a GOD!<br /><br />I have loved every book I have read by Jillian Dodd, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11382346.That_Boy__That_Boy___1_" title="That Boy (That Boy, #1) by Jillian Dodd" rel="nofollow noopener">That Boy</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13361570.That_Wedding__That_Boy___2_" title="That Wedding (That Boy, #2) by Jillian Dodd" rel="nofollow noopener">That Wedding</a>, and all of the Keatyn Chronicles have been 5 stars for me. Dodd gives me the perfect mix of sexual tension, young love, humor, hot sex that isn't overly detailed, but a total turn on, AND there are lots of characters to keep things moving and fresh. I also have Keatyn <i>wardrobe envy</i>! The way Dodd describes Keatyn's clothes with all the top designers make Keatyn a walking fashion statement no matter what the event.<br /><br />Best of all, especially with Keatyn series, Dodd gives me a good healthy dose of anticipation for the next book in the series. I get so frustrated with cliff hangers, but I always feel fulfilled with Dodd's endings and don't mind the wait for the next book. That is weird for me to say because lots of times I delay reading books because of the cliffhanger endings.<br /><br />If you like the New Adult Romance Genre you have to check this series out from the beginning. <br /><br />NOTE** The series also has to be read in order.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7034944510665607291" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_493313092" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/493313092" />
    <a title="Amanda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6293079-amanda"><img alt="Amanda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387657876p2/6293079.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/493313092?book_show_action=true">Jan 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda" href="/user/show/6293079-amanda">Amanda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6293079-amanda?shelf=sequels-to-read">sequels-to-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer493313092" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13082704587484505358">Are you Team Brooklyn? Or,Team Cush? Maybe you’re Team Jake? How about Team Dawson? Let’s not forget the Hottie God himself, Team Aiden! Date Me will keep you holding on by the edge of your seat making you question whose team you really may be on.<br/><br/>Let me first say I had the privilege to beta read this book, and this review is the honest truth.<br/><br/>Date me picks right up where Kiss Me left off. Like, right where it left off. While the story continues with the short time frame, don’t let it fool you. Th</span>
  <span id="freeText13082704587484505358" style="display:none">Are you Team Brooklyn? Or,Team Cush? Maybe you’re Team Jake? How about Team Dawson? Let’s not forget the Hottie God himself, Team Aiden! Date Me will keep you holding on by the edge of your seat making you question whose team you really may be on.<br /><br />Let me first say I had the privilege to beta read this book, and this review is the honest truth.<br /><br />Date me picks right up where Kiss Me left off. Like, right where it left off. While the story continues with the short time frame, don’t let it fool you. This book is far from short and filled to the max of sweet, sassy, and swoon worthy moments. Jillian’s writing style and flow of the story is done to perfection. She sets the pace building up each of the characters- giving us every little detail of what is happening. Jillian gives her readers a deep look into certain characters that will leave you with a jaw dropping expression! There is no piece of information that is not important to this story. <br /><br />Dawson… Oh sweet Dawson. He knows how to bring the heat. Sexual heat that is… <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Dawson is like a sexual buffet. I never know what to expect, what’s going to be next in line. But I definitely want to keep going back for more.'” –Keatyn </i>
</b><br /><br />Aiden. No words can describe how I personally feel about this man. He stepped up his game in Date Me bringing out his more sensitive side. But, let’s not forget about his charming, romantic, sweet, soft, loveable, or charismatic side. We get a deeper look into Aiden’s world, but don’t worry; he still knows how to bring on the flirtatious charm making you squirm in your seat with excitement!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I think being just your friend will be fun.” –Aiden</i>
</b><br /><br />Not only do we get Dallas but we also get the youngest of the Johnson clan, cocky Braxton. And let me tell you, these two are <i>“magically delicious.” </i>Whether it was them bringing their charm, heartfelt advice, or cockiness, they lit up every scene.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“ Dallas: First, I’m gonna ask if she wants to hang out tomorrow night. Then if she puts out, I’ll ask her to HC.<br />Me: DALLAS!!!!<br />Dallas: Cool your orange panties and call me. I won’t try anything but if she attacks me I will NOT resist.”<br /><br />“Braxton: Right now, I’d like a trio of slutty girls. All naked together in my room with nothing to do but me.<br /><br />Me: Let’s try to deal with reality.<br /><br />Braxton: I was. I originally wanted a harem.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Keatyn. I don’t think I could love her more in this book, or yes, be proud. From Stalk Me to Date Me we really get to see a much wiser Keatyn. She is making the right decisions for herself and excepting what comes her way.<br /> <br /><b>
  <i>“But if you have to change for someone, then you are not still you, and that’s bad too. You have to be careful not to lose yourself in the process.” -Keatyn</i>
</b><br /><br />While we get sexual heat, and sweet charm, we also get suspense, thrill, comedy, and heartbreak. Jillian really stepped up her game in Date Me. There were times I was smiling uncontrollably, laughing hard, biting my nails, sweaty palms, and even heart palpitations. Fans of The Keatyn Chronicles will be far from disappointed in this installment. Believe me when I say this is the best in the series and only shows growth in Jillian’s writing and ability. I can only imagine where she will take us in Love Me.<br /><br />~Amanda<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13082704587484505358" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_464425829" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/464425829" />
    <a title="Amy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11654892-amy"><img alt="Amy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1348176924p2/11654892.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/464425829?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy" href="/user/show/11654892-amy">Amy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer464425829" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16277617899631640213">OMG!! OMG!! OMG!!<br/><br/>JUST WOW!!<br/><br/>I cannot even explain how great this series is. If you haven’t read it—YOU NEED TO!! <br/><br/>Date Me starts right where Kiss Me left off. So much stuff happens in this book that my head was spinning—is still spinning. I am not even sure how I feel right now. I loved it. I hated it. I am so torn about it. One thing for sure though is that I am absolutely, no question about it, hooked! Jillian Dodd did such a good job with this book and we really get to see all of the characters</span>
  <span id="freeText16277617899631640213" style="display:none">OMG!! OMG!! OMG!!<br /><br />JUST WOW!!<br /><br />I cannot even explain how great this series is. If you haven’t read it—YOU NEED TO!! <br /><br />Date Me starts right where Kiss Me left off. So much stuff happens in this book that my head was spinning—is still spinning. I am not even sure how I feel right now. I loved it. I hated it. I am so torn about it. One thing for sure though is that I am absolutely, no question about it, hooked! Jillian Dodd did such a good job with this book and we really get to see all of the characters grow a little. <br /><br />K is becoming more of her “true” self. She is opening up to a few people and learning to trust her instincts. She still has a long way to go but I am confident that she is on the right path to discovering and being who she wants to be. Dawes is just so damn sweet and sexy—you can’t help but to like/love him. The chemistry between he and K is undeniable. He is definitely swoon worthy. Aiden is finally starting to show that he has some game where K is concerned. I am really starting to get worried about his potential as Moon Boy. Dallas is still funny as hell and has some of the best pick up lines. I would totally eat Lucky Charms for him—just sayin’. And Riley. Riley…Riley…Riley…If I didn’t love Dawes so much you would be the one babe. Riley is just perfect in this book. He is K’s confidante—she learns she can really trust him and count on him regardless of him being Dawes little brother. He really is her “best” friend and of all the characters I feel he grew the most in this book. I really LOVE him. Of course we still have Whitney the MOLE!!! Oh how I hate thee!! I hope she eventually gets what’s coming to her or seriously grows a heart. The girl is unbelievable! And then there is Damian—good ole’ Damian. Damian is still my pick for Moon Boy if Dawes strikes out—he’s just so loving and caring where K is concerned. Although we didn’t get to see much of him in this book he is there at one of the most important parts and is really sweet to her. Brooklyn isn’t in this book but I know he’ll be back and that has me a little worried in the Moon Boy department.<br /><br />I can’t go into too much detail about this book because so much happens and I don’t want to spoil any second of it. You have to experience it just like I did. And boy was it an experience. I laughed, I cried (boy did I cry) BIG FAT UGLY TEARS, I swooned, and utterly enjoyed it—even though I almost wanted to not finish. My heart couldn’t handle anymore. But I persevered and continued on to the end. I am still just speechless. Well I guess I’m not too speechless because I am writing this review. But WOW is all I can think of to portray my feelings. Regardless of which team you are on I think this is the best book of the series so far. Bravo to Jillian for another fantastic book! Job well done! 5+ Stars!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16277617899631640213" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText5020437597346647217" style="display:none">God where to begin! Lord let me just tell you that Jillian Dodd has me so crazy with this series. This series has had me on a roller coaster of emotions since book one and I can't get off that roller coaster so you will have to read and decide who is right for Keatyn and see who she chooses.               <span id="reviewTextContainer585593379" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1163374767217438101">If Jillian Dodd wrote a novella on bowel movements, I would read it and love it. Jillian Dodd has a great writing style that I can't get enough of. <br/><br/>Keatyn Chronicles are so fun and entertaining! Date Me had me wishing I went to a private high school and wanting to relive my high school years, which is crazy because who wants to relive high school!? Its hard to say, but I think... Date Me is my favorite so FAR (I am holding out for LOVE ME!!!). <br/><br/>TEAM AIDEN all the WAY!!!! </span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('to0xw2pPMMQIMaF3E3s4UOB5HEc2hoAXVxatmbEnJRui259JejQnsrIWRKUM/V85qS6Q+ytSNK2SQd4bspAx/w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NUevJKdZSdkzV6k7dlEvhQI/yytdtrVpxXEDMZCmFN8hEQGutyJer4lwTOlp10jsS2hHl0BiAdMAJnCzkxEAOw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer7393881347602404376">Jillian is a <i>USA TODAY</i> bestselling author who writes fun romance novels with characters her readers fall in love with--from the boy next door in the That Boy trilogy, to the daughter of a famous actress in The Keatyn Chronicles®, to a kick-ass young assassin in the Spy Girl® series.   <span id="freeText7393881347602404376" style="display:none">Jillian is a <i>USA TODAY</i> bestselling author who writes fun romance novels with characters her readers fall in love with--from the boy next door in the That Boy trilogy, to the daughter of a famous actress in The Keatyn Chronicles®, to a kick-ass young assassin in the Spy Girl® series. Jillian's books have enthralled more than two million readers since she burst onto the indie scene in 2011.<br /><br />She lives in a small Florida beach town, is married to her college sweetheart, has two grown children, and two Labrador Retrievers named Cali and Camber. When she's not working, she likes to travel, paint, shop for shoes, watch football, and go to the beach.<br /><br />Check out Jillian’s website for added content: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jilliandodd.net">www.jilliandodd.net</a><br /><br /></span>

        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');
